 	<span class="html-tag">&lt;h2&gt;</span>Remarks<span class="html-tag">&lt;/h2&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="561"></td><td class="line-content">  	<span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">xref</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/api/system.io.streamreader?view=netframework-4.8" rel="noreferrer noopener">system.io.streamreader?view=netframework-4.8</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">data-linktype</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">relative-path</span>"&gt;</span>StreamReader<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> is designed for character input in a particular encoding, whereas the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">xref</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/api/system.io.stream?view=netframework-4.8" rel="noreferrer noopener">system.io.stream?view=netframework-4.8</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">data-linktype</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">relative-path</span>"&gt;</span>Stream<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> class is designed for byte input and output. Use <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">xref</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/api/system.io.streamreader?view=netframework-4.8" rel="noreferrer noopener">system.io.streamreader?view=netframework-4.8</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">data-linktype</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">relative-path</span>"&gt;</span>StreamReader<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> for reading lines of information from a standard text file.  <span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="562"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;div <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">IMPORTANT</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>Important<span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span> This type implements the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">xref</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/api/system.idisposable?view=netframework-4.8" rel="noreferrer noopener">system.idisposable?view=netframework-4.8</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">data-linktype</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">relative-path</span>"&gt;</span>IDisposable<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> interface. When you have finished using the type, you should dispose of it either directly or indirectly. To dispose of the type directly, call its <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">xref</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/api/system.idisposable.dispose?view=netframework-4.8" rel="noreferrer noopener">system.idisposable.dispose?view=netframework-4.8</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">data-linktype</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">relative-path</span>"&gt;</span>Dispose<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> method in a <span class="html-tag">&lt;code&gt;</span>try<span class="html-tag">&lt;/code&gt;</span>/<span class="html-tag">&lt;code&gt;</span>catch<span class="html-tag">&lt;/code&gt;</span> block. To dispose of it indirectly, use a language construct such as <span class="html-tag">&lt;code&gt;</span>using<span class="html-tag">&lt;/code&gt;</span> (in C#) or <span class="html-tag">&lt;code&gt;</span>Using<span class="html-tag">&lt;/code&gt;</span> (in Visual Basic). For more information, see the &amp;quot;Using an Object that Implements IDisposable&amp;quot; section in the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">xref</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/api/system.idisposable?view=netframework-4.8" rel="noreferrer noopener">system.idisposable?view=netframework-4.8</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">data-linktype</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">relative-path</span>"&gt;</span>IDisposable<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> interface topic.  <span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="563"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/div&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="564"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span> <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">xref</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/api/system.io.streamreader?view=netframework-4.8" rel="noreferrer noopener">system.io.streamreader?view=netframework-4.8</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">data-linktype</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">relative-path</span>"&gt;</span>StreamReader<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> defaults to UTF-8 encoding unless specified otherwise, instead of defaulting to the ANSI code page for the current system. UTF-8 handles Unicode characters correctly and provides consistent results on localized versions of the operating system. If you get the current character encoding using the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">xref</span>" <span
